choosing a medspa?","acceptedAnswer":{"@type":"Answer","text":"Physician supervision is the single most important factor. You should ask who the medical director is, their board certification and specialty, and how involved they are in patient care on a daily basis. A physician-supervised medspa provides a higher standard of safety and clinical oversight compared to facilities where physician involvement is primarily administrative. At Rani Beauty Clinic, Dr. Alexander Landfield, a board-certified neurologist, actively oversees all medical treatments."}},{"@type":"Question","name":"How can I evaluate the quality of a medspa's technology?","acceptedAnswer":{"@type":"Answer","text":"Ask about the specific devices and brands the medspa uses, then research those systems. They should include a thorough assessment of your concerns, medical history review, explanation of treatment options, discussion of realistic expectations, and time for your questions. Be cautious of facilities that pressure you to commit to treatment without a proper consultation or that do not take the time to understand your unique goals and health profile."}},{"@type":"Question","name":"Should a medspa offer blood work for medical treatments?","acceptedAnswer":{"@type":"Answer","text":"Yes, if a medspa offers medical treatments like GLP-1 weight management, peptide therapy, or NAD+ injections, they should have the capability to perform and monitor blood work. These treatments interact with your body's physiology and require lab monitoring for safety and effectiveness. Team</p></div><div class="flex items-center gap-4 md:ml-auto"><div class="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-rani-muted"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-calendar" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M8 2v4"></path><path d="M16 2v4"></path><rect width="18" height="18" x="3" y="4" rx="2"></rect><path d="M3 10h18"></path></svg><span class="font-body text-xs">March 8, 2026</span></div><div class="flex items-center gap-1.5"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-tag text-rani-gold" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M12.586 2.586A2 2 0 0 0 11.172 2H4a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v7.172a2 2 0 0 0 .586 1.414l8.704 8.704a2.426 2.426 0 0 0 3.42 0l6.58-6.58a2.426 2.426 0 0 0 0-3.42z"></path><circle cx="7.5" cy="7.5" r=".5" fill="currentColor"></circle></svg><span class="font-body text-xs font-semibold text-rani-navy">Skincare Science</span></div></div></div></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><div class="prose-rani"><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Choosing a medspa is a decision that deserves careful thought. Unlike a traditional spa where the services are primarily relaxation-focused, a medical spa (medspa) offers treatments that involve medical-grade devices, prescription products, and procedures that affect your skin, tissues, and in some cases, your overall health at a physiological level. The treatments available at a medspa, including laser procedures, injectable neuromodulators, dermal fillers, IV therapies, and medical weight management programs, carry real clinical considerations. The quality of the provider, the technology used, and the level of medical oversight can significantly impact not only your results but also your safety.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">If you are looking for a medspa in Renton, WA, or the greater Seattle area, this guide will walk you through the key factors you should evaluate before booking an appointment. These are the same standards we hold ourselves to at Rani Beauty Clinic, and we believe every patient deserves to know what to look for when making this important decision.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Look for Physician Supervision</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">The single most important factor when choosing a medspa is the level of physician oversight involved in your care. In the state of Washington, medspas are required to operate under the supervision of a licensed physician, but the degree of that supervision can vary enormously in practice. At some facilities, a physician&#x27;s name may be on the business paperwork, but they may rarely or never be present at the clinic. At others, a physician is actively involved in treatment planning, patient consultations, and clinical decision-making on a daily basis.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">You should ask directly: Who is the medical director? What is their specialty and board certification? How involved are they in patient care? Is a physician available for questions or concerns during and after your treatment? These are not impolite questions. They are essential ones, and any reputable medspa should answer them transparently.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">At Rani Beauty Clinic, Dr. Alexander Landfield, a board-certified neurologist, serves as our medical director and is actively involved in the clinical oversight of all medical treatments. His presence is not merely administrative. He evaluates patients, develops treatment protocols, supervises medical procedures, and is available for clinical guidance whenever it is needed. This level of physician involvement is what distinguishes a true physician-supervised medspa from facilities that offer medical treatments under more limited oversight.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Check the Technology and Equipment</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">The technology a medspa uses matters enormously. Medical aesthetic devices are not all created equal, and there can be significant differences in effectiveness, safety, and patient comfort between different systems. When evaluating a medspa, ask about the specific devices they use and do some research on those brands and models.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">For laser hair removal, for example, there is a meaningful difference between a high-end, FDA-cleared platform like the Candela GentleMax Pro Plus and a lower-cost device that may not offer the same wavelength options, cooling technology, or treatment customization. The same principle applies to laser skin rejuvenation, body contouring, and other device-based treatments. Premium medical devices represent a significant capital investment for a clinic, and facilities that invest in top-tier technology are generally signaling a commitment to quality and results.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">At Rani Beauty Clinic, we have invested in the Candela GentleMax Pro Plus for laser hair removal, which features dual wavelengths (755nm Alexandrite and 1064nm Nd:YAG) and patented Dynamic Cooling Device technology. This is the same caliber of equipment you would find in top dermatology and plastic surgery practices. We believe our patients deserve access to the best available technology, not older or budget systems that may compromise results or comfort.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Read Reviews and Ask for Before-and-After Photos</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Online reviews and before-and-after photographs provide valuable insight into the real-world experience of a medspa&#x27;s patients. While no review source is perfect, looking at patterns across multiple platforms such as Google, Yelp, and social media can give you a good sense of a clinic&#x27;s strengths and any recurring concerns.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Pay attention to reviews that mention the quality of results, the demeanor of the staff, the cleanliness of the facility, and the overall patient experience. Be wary of clinics with very few reviews or suspiciously uniform five-star ratings. Authentic reviews typically include a mix of detailed experiences that reflect genuine patient interactions.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Before-and-after photos are another helpful tool, especially for treatments like Botox, dermal fillers, laser treatments, and medical weight management. Ask if the clinic can show you photos of their own patients&#x27; results, not stock images provided by the device manufacturer. Real patient results from the actual clinic give you the most accurate picture of what you can expect.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Ask About Credentials and Training</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">The credentials of the people performing your treatments are just as important as the technology they use. Ask about the qualifications of the injectors, laser technicians, and other staff members. What certifications do they hold? What is their training background? How many procedures have they performed? Do they participate in ongoing education and training?</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">For injectable treatments like Botox, Dysport, and dermal fillers, the skill and experience of the injector directly impacts the quality of your results. Injecting neuromodulators and fillers is as much an art as it is a science, requiring detailed knowledge of facial anatomy, product properties, and aesthetic principles. A provider who has performed hundreds or thousands of injections will generally deliver more consistent, refined results than someone who is newer to the field.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">For laser procedures, the technician&#x27;s familiarity with the specific device, their ability to customize treatment parameters for different skin types and concerns, and their training in managing potential complications are all critical factors. At Rani Beauty Clinic, our team members are highly trained on the specific equipment we use and follow evidence-based treatment protocols developed under Dr. Landfield&#x27;s clinical guidance.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Ensure Thorough Consultations Are Standard Practice</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">A high-quality medspa will never rush you into a treatment without a proper consultation. Your first visit should include a thorough assessment of your concerns, a review of your medical history, an explanation of the recommended treatment options, a discussion of realistic expectations, and an opportunity to ask questions.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Be cautious of any facility that pressures you to commit to treatment during your first visit or that does not take the time to understand your individual needs and goals. A consultation is not just a sales opportunity. It is a clinical evaluation that helps ensure the recommended treatment is appropriate and safe for you specifically. At Rani Beauty Clinic, we prioritize consultations because we believe informed patients make better decisions and achieve better outcomes.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">You should also feel comfortable and welcome during your consultation. The environment of the clinic, the attentiveness of the staff, and the willingness of the provider to answer your questions all contribute to the overall quality of your care. Trust your instincts. If something feels rushed, dismissive, or overly sales-driven, that may be a red flag about the quality of care you can expect during treatment.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Verify Blood Work Capabilities for Medical Treatments</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">If you are considering medical treatments such as GLP-1 weight management, peptide therapy, hormone optimization, or NAD+ injections, it is essential that the medspa has the capability to perform and monitor blood work. These are not purely cosmetic procedures. They involve medications and therapies that interact with your body&#x27;s physiology, and proper lab monitoring is necessary to ensure both safety and effectiveness.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Ask whether the clinic performs blood work on-site or requires you to visit an external laboratory. On-site blood work is a significant convenience that can streamline your treatment timeline and improve adherence to monitoring protocols. More importantly, ask how the results are reviewed and integrated into your treatment plan. Lab work should not be a checkbox exercise. It should be a meaningful clinical tool that informs your provider&#x27;s decisions about dosing, medication selection, and ongoing adjustments.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">At Rani Beauty Clinic, we offer in-house blood work, which means you can have your labs drawn during the same visit as your consultation. Results are reviewed by Dr. Landfield and used to develop and refine your personalized treatment plan. This integrated approach ensures that medical treatments are grounded in objective clinical data rather than guesswork.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Consider the Full Range of Services</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">A medspa that offers a comprehensive range of services can be advantageous because it means you can address multiple concerns under one roof with a team that understands your full health and aesthetic picture. When your Botox provider also knows about your skincare routine, your laser treatments, and any wellness therapies you are receiving, they can coordinate your care more effectively and identify potential interactions or contraindications.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">At Rani Beauty Clinic, we offer a full spectrum of aesthetic treatments including Botox, Dysport, laser hair removal, HydraFacial, and microneedling, alongside medical wellness services such as GLP-1 weight management, peptide therapy, NAD+ injections, and vitamin injections. This breadth of services allows us to take a holistic approach to each patient&#x27;s care, addressing both aesthetic goals and overall health and wellness within a single, physician-supervised practice.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Making Your Decision</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">Choosing a medspa is ultimately about finding a provider you trust to deliver safe, effective, and personalized care. The factors we have discussed, physician supervision, technology, reviews, credentials, consultations, and blood work capabilities, provide a practical framework for evaluating your options. Take the time to visit the clinic, meet the team, and ask questions. The right medspa will welcome your inquiry and earn your confidence through transparency, expertise, and genuine care for your wellbeing.</p><p class="mb-6 font-body text-base leading-[1.85] text-rani-text">If you would like to learn more about Rani Beauty Clinic or schedule a consultation, we invite you to visit our contact page at /contact. Our team is here to answer your questions and help you make an informed decision about your aesthetic and wellness care.</p></div></div><div style="opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)"><div
